{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01Lzv1ssWCh6QVoFWvKJgYk2","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_014jGPsREkBx4PsovF1dnJXH","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Prometheus TSDB Compaction Operational Runbook\n\n## 1. Overview\n\n### What is TSDB Compaction?\n\nTSDB compaction is the process of merging multiple time series data blocks into larger, more efficient blocks while removing deleted series and optimizing storage layout. Compaction maintains query performance and manages disk space in Prometheus's time series database.\n\n**Key objectives:**\n- Merge overlapping time blocks to prevent duplicate data in queries\n- Remove tombstoned (deleted) series to reclaim disk space\n- Consolidate smaller blocks into larger ones following an exponential leveling strategy\n- Optimize chunk sizes and index structure for better query performance\n\n### Block Structure\n\nBlocks are immutable, self-contained units of time series data. Each block:\n- Contains data for a specific time range `[MinTime, MaxTime)`\n- Is stored as a directory with `meta.json`, chunks, index, and tombstones files\n- Is identified by a ULID (Universally Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifier)\n- Has a compaction level indicating how many times it has been compacted\n- Tracks parent blocks and source ULIDs for debugging and recovery\n\n**Block organization:**\n```\ntsdb_data/\n├── 01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV/  # Block ULID\n│   ├── meta.json                 # Metadata: time range, stats, compaction info\n│   ├── index                     # Index of all series and labels\n│   ├── chunks/                   # Chunk segment files\n│   └── tombstones                # Deletion markers\n├── 01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ70G5FAW/\n...\n├── wal/                          # Write-ahead log (active head)\n└── wbl/                          # Write-ahead log for out-of-order samples\n```\n\n### Compaction Levels and Exponential Ranges\n\nPrometheus uses exponential block ranges to organize compaction:\n- **Level 1**: Head block (in-memory) → first persistent block (2 hours by default)\n- **Level 2**: Merge 2-4 level 1 blocks → 6-hour block\n- **Level 3**: Merge level 2 blocks → 18-hour block\n- **Level N**: Each higher level blocks merge based on exponential progression\n\nDefault ranges with `MinBlockDuration = 2h` and `MaxBlockDuration = 2h`:\n```\nRange 0:  2 hours\nRange 1:  6 hours (2h × 3)\nRange 2:  18 hours (6h × 3)\nRange 3:  54 hours (18h × 3)\n...continuing exponentially...\n```\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\n**1. Time-based Trigger (Primary)**\n- Triggered automatically every minute by the compaction loop in `db.go:993-1027`\n- Runs when the head block is \"compactable\" (older than `chunkRange/2`)\n- Ensures timely persistence of in-memory data to disk\n\n**2. Size-based Trigger**\n- Head block is compacted when it reaches a size threshold\n- Determined by `db.head.compactable()` check in `head.go`\n\n**3. Appender-based Trigger**\n- Triggered on `Appender.Commit()` if head is compactable\n- Provides immediate notification of compactable blocks\n\n**4. Tombstone Cleanup Trigger**\n- Blocks with >5% tombstones are automatically compacted to remove deleted series (line 281 in `compact.go`)\n- Saves disk space by eliminating deletion markers\n\n**5. Overlapping Blocks Trigger**\n- If blocks overlap, they are immediately compacted together for correctness\n- Prevents query inconsistencies from overlapping time ranges\n\n### Compaction Process Flow\n\n```\n1. Trigger (time, size, or tombstone threshold)\n   ↓\n2. Acquire Compaction Mutex (cmtx)\n   ↓\n3. Compact Head Block (if compactable)\n   a. Create RangeHead wrapping the head\n   b. Write head to disk as level-1 block\n   c. Reload blocks and delete parents\n   ↓\n4. Compact Disk Blocks (multiple iterations)\n   a. Plan: Compactor.Plan() identifies compactable block groups\n   b. Compact: Merge identified blocks\n   c. Write: Create new compacted block\n   d. Reload: Update in-memory block list\n   e. Delete: Remove source blocks\n   ↓\n5. WAL Truncation (optional)\n   ↓\n6. Release Compaction Mutex\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Metrics to Watch\n\n#### Compaction Execution Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | N/A (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Total triggered compactions | Increase rate >1/min may indicate high data churn |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compactions (excluding cancellations) | **ALERT: ANY increase** indicates compaction failures |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Time taken per compaction | p99 > 5min indicates slow compaction |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | 1 = block being written, 0 = idle | Should be 0 most of the time |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | High rate indicates frequent overlaps |\n\n#### Block and Storage Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Number of on-disk blocks loaded in memory | >100 suggests compaction not keeping pace |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Total on-disk block storage size | Compare to `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Max bytes to retain (configured) | N/A (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_seconds` | Gauge | Max retention duration (configured) | N/A (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes` | Gauge | In-memory symbol table size | >500MB indicates many unique labels |\n\n#### Retention Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_time_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted due to time retention | Increase rate >0.5/hour may indicate aggressive retention |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_size_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted due to size retention | Increase indicates hitting size limits |\n\n#### Chunk Metrics (Level 1 compaction)\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes` | Histogram | Final chunk size on first compaction | p50 < 100 bytes = inefficient chunking |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples` | Histogram | Samples per chunk on first compaction | p50 > 500 samples = good compression |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds` | Histogram | Time range covered per chunk | Should align with scrape intervals |\n\n#### Tombstone Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds` | Histogram | Time to recompact blocks and remove tombstones | p99 > 10min indicates heavy deletions |\n\n### Healthy Compaction Indicators\n\n✅ **Good signs:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` is **stable** (not increasing)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` p99 < 5 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` gradually increases then stabilizes after compaction\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` stays near configured retention limit\n- Compactions triggered roughly once per block duration (e.g., every 2 hours)\n\n### Unhealthy Compaction Indicators\n\n⚠️ **Warning signs:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` **increasing** → investigate logs\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` **always increasing** → compaction not keeping pace\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` p99 > 10 minutes → system under stress\n- Logs showing \"compact %s: failed\" or \"compaction failed: %v\" → active failure\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` exceeds `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` consistently\n\n### Alert Examples\n\n```yaml\n# Critical: Compaction Failures\n- alert: TSDBCompactionFailing\n  expr: rate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[5m]) > 0\n  for: 10m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"Prometheus TSDB compaction failing on {{ $labels.job }}\"\n    description: \"Compactions have failed {{ $value }} times in last 5 minutes\"\n\n# Warning: Compaction Too Slow\n- alert: TSDBCompactionSlow\n  expr: histogram_quantile(0.99, prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds) > 300\n  for: 20m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"Prometheus TSDB compaction slow on {{ $labels.job }}\"\n    description: \"p99 compaction duration is {{ $value }}s (threshold: 300s)\"\n\n# Warning: Too Many Blocks\n- alert: TSDBTooManyBlocks\n  expr: prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded > 100\n  for: 30m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"Too many blocks loaded on {{ $labels.job }}\"\n    description: \"{{ $value }} blocks loaded (compaction may not be keeping pace)\"\n\n# Warning: Storage Growing Beyond Retention\n- alert: TSDBSizeRetention\n  expr: prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes > prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes\n  for: 1h\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"TSDB storage exceeds retention limit on {{ $labels.job }}\"\n    description: \"Storage {{ $value }}B exceeds limit {{ $value }}B\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes and Diagnostics\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus crashes with \"no space left on device\" error\n- Compaction metrics stop updating\n- WAL or new blocks cannot be written\n- Logs show: `\"write merged meta: %w\"`, `\"sync temporary dir file: %w\"`, or `\"rename block dir: %w\"`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases sharply\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Retention settings too loose (time or size-based)\n- WAL not being truncated after compaction\n- Retention parameters misconfigured or not applied\n- Unexpected data ingestion spike\n- Other processes consuming disk space\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. **Check disk space:**\n   ```bash\n   df -h /prometheus-data-dir\n   du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/*\n   ```\n\n2. **Verify retention configuration:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect --metrics /prometheus-data-dir\n   # Look for block age and size\n   ls -lh /prometheus-data-dir | grep -E '^d' | head -20\n   ```\n\n3. **Check block metadata:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect --metrics /prometheus-data-dir | tail -20\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor compaction logs:**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch for \"compact blocks\" or \"compact blocks resulted in empty block\" messages\n   grep -i \"compact\\|delete\" /prometheus-logs/prometheus.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n5. **Inspect WAL size:**\n   ```bash\n   du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/wal\n   du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/wbl  # Out-of-order WAL if present\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Block deletion logic: `tsdb/db.go:1652-1683` (deleteBlocks)\n- Retention enforcement: `tsdb/db.go:1568-1649` (deletableBlocks, BeyondTimeRetention, BeyondSizeRetention)\n- Compaction write: `tsdb/compact.go:606-717` (write function)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Compaction runs but never completes (hanging processes)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` increases but `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` does not\n- Blocks accumulate; `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` continuously increases\n- Compaction log messages appear periodically but then stop\n- Out-of-memory errors or heavy CPU/disk I/O during compaction\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Compaction context cancelled due to shutdown or signal (lines 1158-1160 in db.go)\n- Query locks preventing block reloading after compaction\n- Corrupted block preventing reload (lines 1441-1477 in db.go)\n- Insufficient memory for merging large blocks\n- Disk I/O bottleneck causing timeout\n- Concurrent compaction mutex contention\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. **Check compaction loop status:**\n   ```bash\n   # Prometheus metrics endpoint\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep -i compaction\n   ```\n\n2. **Inspect goroutines and locks:**\n   ```bash\n   # Via pprof\n   curl -s http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/goroutine | head -100\n   curl -s http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/mutex | head -100\n   ```\n\n3. **Monitor block loading:**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch for reloadBlocks errors\n   grep -i \"reloadBlocks\\|failed to reloadBlocks\" /prometheus-logs/prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n4. **Check for corrupted blocks:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data-dir 2>&1 | grep -i corrupt\n   # Or check each block's meta.json\n   for block in /prometheus-data-dir/*/meta.json; do\n     echo \"Checking $block\"\n     cat \"$block\" | jq .\n   done\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor system resources:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check during compaction\n   top -b -n1 | grep prometheus\n   iostat -x 1 10\n   free -h\n   ```\n\n6. **Enable debug logging:**\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/-/reload  # Reload config after adding debug level\n   # Or restart with --log.level=debug\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Compaction context handling: `tsdb/db.go:1008-1026`, `tsdb/compact.go:659-663`\n- Block reloading: `tsdb/db.go:1424-1529` (reloadBlocks)\n- Mutex locking: `tsdb/db.go:1134-1135` (Compact function lock)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption or Invalid Metadata\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Error messages: `\"Failed to read meta.json\"`, `\"corrupted block\"`, `\"unexpected meta file version\"`\n- Corrupted blocks marked for deletion but not fully removed\n- Queries fail with \"block not found\" or index corruption errors\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increments\n- Logs show: `\"Found corrupted block\"` (line 1474 in db.go)\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Disk corruption (bit rot, bad sector)\n- Abrupt process termination during block write (lines 712-715 in compact.go)\n- Filesystem error or unmapped device\n- Atomic rename failed (partial block write)\n- Incompatible version upgrade/downgrade\n- Manual block manipulation outside Prometheus\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. **List and inspect block metadata:**\n   ```bash\n   # Identify corrupted blocks\n   for block_dir in /prometheus-data-dir/*/; do\n     if ! cat \"$block_dir/meta.json\" 2>/dev/null | jq . >/dev/null; then\n       echo \"CORRUPTED: $(basename $block_dir)\"\n       ls -la \"$block_dir\"\n     fi\n   done\n   ```\n\n2. **Check filesystem integrity:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check for filesystem errors\n   fsck -n /dev/prometheus-device  # Read-only check\n   # Check if device is mounted read-only\n   mount | grep prometheus-data-dir\n   ```\n\n3. **Inspect block structure:**\n   ```bash\n   # For a suspect block\n   block_id=\"01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV\"\n   cd /prometheus-data-dir/$block_id\n   ls -la\n\n   # Check index file\n   file index\n\n   # Check chunks\n   ls -la chunks/\n\n   # Validate meta.json JSON syntax\n   jq . meta.json\n   ```\n\n4. **Check for incomplete compactions:**\n   ```bash\n   # Look for .tmp-for-creation or .tmp-for-deletion directories\n   find /prometheus-data-dir -name \"*tmp*\" -type d\n   # These should be cleaned up automatically; if they persist, manual cleanup needed\n   ```\n\n5. **Disk integrity test:**\n   ```bash\n   # Verify block files with checksums (if available)\n   cd /prometheus-data-dir\n   find . -type f -name \"index\" -o -name \"chunks/*\" | xargs md5sum > checksums.txt\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Meta file reading: `tsdb/block.go:247-262` (readMetaFile)\n- Meta file writing: `tsdb/block.go:264-299` (writeMetaFile)\n- Atomic block rename: `tsdb/compact.go:712-715` (fileutil.Replace)\n- Block opening: `tsdb/block.go:328-390` (OpenBlock)\n- Corruption detection: `tsdb/db.go:1463-1477` (corrupted blocks handling)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Process killed by OS (exit code 137 on Linux)\n- Kernel logs show: `\"Killed process ... (prometheus) total-vm ... rss ...\"`\n- Sudden Prometheus restart with no error logs\n- Compaction metrics show spike in `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` before crash\n- Large blocks fail to compact (e.g., blocks with millions of series)\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Compacting very large blocks with millions of series (lines 729-800 in compact.go)\n- Symbol table loading consumes excessive memory (line 272-284 in db.go)\n- Index reader keeping all label pairs in memory\n- Chunk merging for overlapping blocks with duplicate data\n- System has insufficient RAM for Prometheus heap\n- Memory leak in chunk pool or block readers\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. **Monitor memory usage:**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch real-time memory\n   watch -n 5 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep'\n\n   # Get process memory stats\n   cat /proc/$(pgrep prometheus)/status | grep -E \"VmPeak|VmHWM|VmRSS\"\n   ```\n\n2. **Check block sizes before compaction:**\n   ```bash\n   # Find largest blocks\n   du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/*/ | sort -h | tail -10\n\n   # Inspect block metadata\n   for d in $(du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/*/ | sort -rh | head -5 | awk '{print $2}'); do\n     echo \"Block: $d\"\n     jq '.stats, .compaction.level' \"$d/meta.json\"\n   done\n   ```\n\n3. **Check symbol table size:**\n   ```bash\n   # Via metrics\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size\n\n   # Query the count of unique label combinations\n   promtool tsdb inspect --metrics /prometheus-data-dir | grep -i symbol\n   ```\n\n4. **Review Prometheus heap configuration:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check startup parameters\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n\n   # Current memory limit\n   ulimit -m  # Memory limit\n   ulimit -v  # Virtual memory\n   ```\n\n5. **Analyze compaction targets:**\n   ```bash\n   # Simulate compaction planning\n   promtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data-dir\n   # Look for very large or high-level blocks that would be merged\n   ```\n\n6. **Enable memory profiling:**\n   ```bash\n   # Via pprof\n   curl -s http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/heap > heap.prof\n   go tool pprof heap.prof\n   # In pprof: top10, list [function_name]\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Block population (merging): `tsdb/compact.go:729-850` (PopulateBlock)\n- Symbol table loading: `tsdb/db.go:272-284` (symbol table metrics)\n- Index reading: `tsdb/index/` package\n- Chunk pool management: `tsdb/chunkenc/pool.go`\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 5: WAL Truncation Failure\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- WAL directory grows unboundedly (`/prometheus-data-dir/wal` > 5GB)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_wal_corruptions_total` increases (indicates potential corruption)\n- Logs show: `\"WAL truncation in Compact\"`, `\"truncate WAL: %w\"`\n- Startup takes increasingly long (WAL replay is slow)\n- Metrics show normal compaction but WAL not being cleaned\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- WAL segments locked by concurrent readers (line 1147 in db.go)\n- Permission issues on WAL directory\n- Out-of-order head compaction preventing WAL truncation (lines 1205-1209 in db.go)\n- Last block max time not advancing (broken compaction chain)\n- Concurrent checkpoint/truncation operations\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. **Check WAL directory size:**\n   ```bash\n   du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/wal\n   ls -lh /prometheus-data-dir/wal | head -20\n\n   # Count WAL segments\n   ls /prometheus-data-dir/wal | wc -l\n   # Expected: ~3-5 files; >10 indicates truncation failure\n   ```\n\n2. **Inspect WAL file locks:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check open file handles\n   lsof | grep prometheus | grep wal\n\n   # Check memory-mapped files\n   cat /proc/$(pgrep prometheus)/maps | grep wal\n   ```\n\n3. **Verify block time progression:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check newest block's MaxTime\n   latest_block=$(ls -1 /prometheus-data-dir | grep -v wal | grep -v wbl | sort -r | head -1)\n   cat /prometheus-data-dir/$latest_block/meta.json | jq '.maxTime'\n\n   # Compare with expected time (should be recent)\n   echo \"Current time (ms): $(date +%s)000\"\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor OOO head compaction:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check if OOO head compaction is blocked\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep -i \"out_of_order\"\n\n   # Look for OOO blocks\n   ls /prometheus-data-dir/*/meta.json | xargs grep -l \"from-out-of-order\"\n   ```\n\n5. **Check filesystem and permissions:**\n   ```bash\n   ls -ld /prometheus-data-dir/wal\n   # Should show: drwx------ prometheus prometheus\n\n   # Test write permission\n   touch /prometheus-data-dir/wal/test && rm /prometheus-data-dir/wal/test\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- WAL truncation in compaction: `tsdb/db.go:1147-1150`, `tsdb/db.go:1192-1194`\n- OOO head compaction: `tsdb/db.go:1238-1283`\n- Head truncation: `tsdb/head.go` (head.truncateWAL method)\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### Recovery Procedure for Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Step 1: Stop Prometheus immediately**\n```bash\n# Gracefully shut down Prometheus to prevent data loss\n# If possible, give it 30 seconds to finish current operations\nkill -SIGTERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 30\n\n# If not stopping, force kill\nkill -SIGKILL $(pgrep prometheus)\n```\n\n**Step 2: Assess free disk space**\n```bash\ndf -h /prometheus-data-dir\n# Need at least 5GB free to safely restart compaction\ndu -sh /prometheus-data-dir/*\n```\n\n**Step 3: Delete old blocks manually if needed (last resort)**\n```bash\n# List blocks sorted by age (oldest first)\nls -lt /prometheus-data-dir | grep -v wal | grep -v wbl | tail -20\n\n# Identify ULID of oldest block to delete\noldest_block=\"01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV\"\n\n# Delete with atomic rename pattern (safe)\nmv /prometheus-data-dir/$oldest_block /prometheus-data-dir/${oldest_block}.tmp-for-deletion\nrm -rf /prometheus-data-dir/${oldest_block}.tmp-for-deletion\n\n# Verify deletion\nls /prometheus-data-dir/$oldest_block 2>&1 | grep \"No such file\"\n\n# Repeat for multiple blocks as needed\n```\n\n**Step 4: Clean up orphaned temporary directories**\n```bash\n# Remove any incomplete compaction artifacts\nfind /prometheus-data-dir -name \"*tmp*\" -type d -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null || true\n```\n\n**Step 5: Adjust retention if needed**\n```bash\n# Update prometheus.yml retention settings:\n# storage:\n#   tsdb:\n#     retention.time: 7d        # Reduce from 15d to 7d\n#     retention.size: 50GB      # Add or reduce size-based limit\n\n# Then reload:\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/reload\n```\n\n**Step 6: Restart Prometheus**\n```bash\n# Start with reduced retention temporarily\nprometheus --storage.tsdb.retention.time=7d --storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus-data-dir\n\n# Monitor startup logs\n# Watch for: \"completed write to block\" messages indicating compaction\n```\n\n**Step 7: Monitor compaction and disk space**\n```bash\n# Terminal 1: Watch metrics\nwatch -n 10 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep -E \"compactions|blocks|storage\"'\n\n# Terminal 2: Watch disk space\nwatch -n 10 'df -h /prometheus-data-dir && echo \"---\" && du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/*/ | sort -h'\n\n# Terminal 3: Monitor logs\ntail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -i \"compact\\|delete\\|retain\"\n```\n\n**Step 8: Verify recovery**\n```bash\n# Check that compactions are progressing\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n\n# Verify storage is decreasing\nwatch -n 60 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes'\n\n# Ensure no failures\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total\n# Should show 0 or stable value\n```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery Procedure for Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck\n\n**Step 1: Identify if compaction is truly stuck**\n```bash\n# Check if metrics are updating\nfor i in {1..5}; do\n  curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n  sleep 10\ndone\n# If value doesn't change, compaction is stuck\n\n# Check if Prometheus process is running\nps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\npgrep -f prometheus\n```\n\n**Step 2: Attempt graceful shutdown with timeout**\n```bash\n# Send SIGTERM and wait\ntimeout 60 bash -c 'kill -SIGTERM $(pgrep prometheus) && wait $(pgrep prometheus)'\n\n# If timeout expires, process is hung - force kill\nif [ $? -eq 124 ]; then\n  kill -SIGKILL $(pgrep prometheus)\n  sleep 5\nfi\n```\n\n**Step 3: Check for incomplete compactions**\n```bash\n# Look for blocks in tmp directories (incomplete writes)\nfind /prometheus-data-dir -name \"*tmp*\" -type d -ls\n\n# Check if any .tmp-for-creation or .tmp-for-deletion directories exist\nls -la /prometheus-data-dir/*tmp* 2>/dev/null || echo \"No tmp directories found\"\n```\n\n**Step 4: Validate block metadata integrity**\n```bash\n# For each block, validate meta.json\nerrors=0\nfor block in /prometheus-data-dir/*/; do\n  if [ -f \"$block/meta.json\" ]; then\n    if ! jq . \"$block/meta.json\" >/dev/null 2>&1; then\n      echo \"INVALID JSON: $(basename $block)\"\n      ((errors++))\n    fi\n  fi\ndone\n\nif [ $errors -gt 0 ]; then\n  echo \"Found $errors blocks with invalid meta.json\"\n  # Proceed to Failure Mode 3 recovery\nelse\n  echo \"All block metadata valid\"\nfi\n```\n\n**Step 5: Restart Prometheus with compaction disabled (if needed)**\n```bash\n# Use this only if compaction causes repeated hangs\nprometheus \\\n  --storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus-data-dir \\\n  --storage.tsdb.allow-overlapping-blocks \\\n  > /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log 2>&1 &\n\n# Wait for startup\nsleep 30\n\n# Verify it stays alive\nsleep 30 && pgrep -f prometheus >/dev/null && echo \"Prometheus running\"\n```\n\n**Step 6: Manually trigger compaction with timeout**\n```bash\n# If Prometheus is running, try triggering via API\n# (Note: may not be available in all versions, check documentation)\n\n# Alternative: Restart to force compaction loop\nkill -SIGTERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 60\n\n# Start normally\nprometheus --storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus-data-dir &\n\n# Monitor with timeout\ntimeout 600 bash -c 'while true; do\n  compacted=$(curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics 2>/dev/null | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total | grep -oE \"[0-9]+$\")\n  [ -n \"$compacted\" ] && echo \"Last compaction: $compacted\"\n  sleep 30\ndone'\n```\n\n**Step 7: If still stuck after restart, use promtool**\n```bash\n# Stop Prometheus\nkill -SIGTERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 10\n\n# Run promtool to check and repair\npromtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data-dir\n\n# If errors found, attempt repair\npromtool tsdb repair /prometheus-data-dir\n\n# Then restart\nprometheus --storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus-data-dir &\n```\n\n**Step 8: Monitor and verify**\n```bash\n# Watch compaction progress\nwatch -n 30 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep -E \"compactions_total|blocks_loaded|compaction_duration\"'\n\n# Check logs for errors\ntail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -i \"compact\\|error\"\n```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery Procedure for Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Step 1: Identify corrupted blocks**\n```bash\n# Full validation of all corrupted_blocks+=(\"$block_id\")\n  fi\ndone\n\necho \"Corrupted blocks: ${#corrupted_blocks[@]}\"\n```\n\n**Step 2: Stop Prometheus**\n```bash\n# Graceful shutdown\nkill -SIGTERM $(pgrep Code Reference\n\n### Key Functions by Failure Mode\n\n#### Disk Space Exhaustion\n- **Block deletion**: `tsdb/db.go:1652-1683` - `deleteBlocks()`\n- **Retention calculation**: `tsdb/db.go:1568-1649` - `deletableBlocks()`, `BeyondTimeRetention()`, `BeyondSizeRetention()`\n- **Compaction write**: `tsdb/compact.go:606-717` - `write()` method\n- **Block atomicity**: `tsdb/block.go:264-299` - `writeMetaFile()`\n\n#### Compaction Stuck\n- **Compaction loop**: `tsdb/db.go:993-1027` - main compaction loop with triggering\n- **Mutex handling**: `tsdb/db.go:1134-1135` - `Compact()` lock acquisition\n- **Context cancellation**: `tsdb/db.go:1158-1160` - context cancel handling\n- **Block reload**: `tsdb/db.go:1424-1529` - `reloadBlocks()`\n\n#### Block Corruption\n- **Meta file reading**: `tsdb/block.go:247-262` - `readMetaFile()`\n- **Meta file writing**: `tsdb/block.go:264-299` - `writeMetaFile()`\n- **Block opening**: `tsdb/block.go:328-390` - `OpenBlock()`\n- **Atomic rename**: `tsdb/compact.go:712-715` - `fileutil.Replace()`\n\n#### Out-of-Memory\n- **Block population**: `tsdb/compact.go:729-850` - `PopulateBlock()`\n- **Symbol table**: `tsdb/db.go:272-284` - symbol table metrics and loading\n- **Chunk merging**: `tsdb/compact.go:800-850` - merging chunks in compaction\n\n#### WAL Truncation\n- **WAL truncation**: `tsdb/db.go:1147-1150`, `1192-1194` - WAL truncation calls\n- **OOO compaction**: `tsdb/db.go:1238-1283` - `compactOOOHead()`\n- **Head truncation**: `tsdb/head.go` - `truncateWAL()` and `truncateMemory()` methods\n\n### Important Types and Constants\n\n```go\n// Block metadata structure (tsdb/block.go:162-179)\ntype BlockMeta struct {\n    ULID        ulid.ULID\n    MinTime, MaxTime int64\n    Stats       BlockStats\n    Compaction  BlockMetaCompaction\n    Version     int\n}\n\n// Compaction metadata (tsdb/block.go:196-212)\ntype BlockMetaCompaction struct {\n    Level      int         // 1, 2, 3, ... (higher = more compacted)\n    Sources    []ulid.ULID // Head ULIDs that went into this block\n    Deletable  bool        // Mark for deletion\n    Parents    []BlockDesc // Direct source blocks\n    Failed     bool        // Compaction of source blocks failed\n    Hints      []string    // \"from-out-of-order\", etc.\n}\n\n// Compaction constants\nconst (\n    tmpForDeletionBlockDirSuffix = \".tmp-for-deletion\"\n    tmpForCreationBlockDirSuffix  = \".tmp-for-creation\"\n)\n\n// Default block durations\nconst DefaultBlockDuration = 2 * time.Hour // 7200000 milliseconds\n```\n\n### Monitoring and Debugging Commands\n\n```bash\n# Check compaction status via metrics\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compaction\n\n# Inspect TSDB using promtool\npromtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data-dir\n\n# Repair TSDB\npromtool tsdb repair /prometheus-data-dir\n\n# Enable debug logging\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/reload  # After updating log level in config\n\n# Profile heap during OOM issue\ncurl -s http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/heap > heap.prof\ngo tool pprof heap.prof\n\n# Analyze goroutines for stuck compactions\ncurl -s http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/goroutine?debug=2 | grep -A 20 \"Compact\\|compact\"\n```\n\n### Recovery Script Template\n\n```bash\n#!/bin/bash\n# Prometheus TSDB Compaction Recovery Script\nset -e\n\nPROMETHEUS_DIR=\"/prometheus-data-dir\"\nPROMETHEUS_PID=$(pgrep prometheus || true)\nBACKUP_DIR=\"/backup/tsdb-recovery-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)\"\n\necho \"Starting TSDB recovery...\"\necho \"TSDB directory: $PROMETHEUS_DIR\"\necho \"Backup directory: $BACKUP_DIR\"\n\n# 1. Clean temporary files\nfind \"$PROMETHEUS_DIR\" -name \"*tmp*\" -type d -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null || true\n\n# 5. Restart Prometheus\necho \"Restarting Prometheus...\"\nprometheus --storage.tsdb.path=\"$PROMETHEUS_DIR\" > /var/log/prometheus/recovery.log 2>&1 &\n\n# 6. Monitor recovery\nsleep 30\nfor i in {1..30}; do\n    if curl -s http://localhost:9090/-/healthy 2>/dev/null | grep -q \"Prometheus is healthy\"; then\n        echo \"Prometheus recovered successfully!\"\n        break\n    fi\n    echo \"Waiting for Prometheus recovery... ($i/30)\"\n    sleep 10\ndone\n\necho \"Recovery complete. Backup saved to: $BACKUP_DIR\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThis runbook provides operational guidance for managing Prometheus TSDB compaction in production. Key takeaways:\n\n1. **Monitor actively**: Watch `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total`, `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded`, and `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds`\n2. **Plan retention**: Configure time and size-based retention to prevent disk exhaustion\n3. **Respond quickly**: Compaction failures require immediate investigation and restart\n4. **Backup regularly**: Maintain backups before manual recovery operations\n5. **Keep logs**: Save Prometheus logs during incidents for post-mortem analysis\n\nFor further information, consult:\n- Prometheus documentation: https://prometheus.io/docs/prometheus/latest/storage/\n- TSDB source code: `tsdb/` directory in Prometheus repository\n- Community issues: GitHub prometheus/prometheus issues and discussions\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3649,"cache_read_input_tokens":85252,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3649},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e2a23fc2-bfa0-4326-b775-78ccfd51d975","uuid":"bb2610fe-acb9-4e01-8a5c-bfc0e2d59eee"}

Overview\n\n### What is TSDB Compaction?\n\nTSDB compaction is the process of merging multiple time series data blocks into larger, more efficient blocks while removing deleted series and optimizing storage layout. Compaction maintains query performance and manages disk space in Prometheus's time series database.\n\n**Key objectives:**\n- Merge overlapping time blocks to prevent duplicate data in queries\n- Remove tombstoned (deleted) series to reclaim disk space\n- Consolidate smaller blocks into larger ones following an exponential leveling strategy\n- Optimize chunk sizes and index structure for better query performance\n\n### Block Structure\n\nBlocks are immutable, self-contained units of time series data. Each block:\n- Contains data for a specific time range `[MinTime, MaxTime)`\n- Is stored as a directory with `meta.json`, chunks, index, and tombstones files\n- Is identified by a ULID (Universally Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifier)\n- Has a compaction level indicating how many times it has been compacted\n- Tracks parent blocks and source ULIDs for debugging and recovery\n\n**Block organization:**\n```\ntsdb_data/\n├── 01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV/  # Block ULID\n│   ├── meta.json                 # Metadata: time range, stats, compaction info\n│   ├── index                     # Index of all series and labels\n│   ├── chunks/                   # Chunk segment files\n│   └── tombstones                # Deletion markers\n├── 01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ70G5FAW/\n...\n├── wal/                          # Write-ahead log (active head)\n└── wbl/                          # Write-ahead log for out-of-order samples\n```\n\n### Compaction Levels and Exponential Ranges\n\nPrometheus uses exponential block ranges to organize compaction:\n- **Level 1**: Head block (in-memory) → first persistent block (2 hours by default)\n- **Level 2**: Merge 2-4 level 1 blocks → 6-hour block\n- **Level 3**: Merge level 2 blocks → 18-hour block\n- **Level N**: Each higher level blocks merge based on exponential progression\n\nDefault ranges with `MinBlockDuration = 2h` and `MaxBlockDuration = 2h`:\n```\nRange 0:  2 hours\nRange 1:  6 hours (2h × 3)\nRange 2:  18 hours (6h × 3)\nRange 3:  54 hours (18h × 3)\n...continuing exponentially...\n```\n\n### When Compaction is Triggered\n\n**1. Time-based Trigger (Primary)**\n- Triggered automatically every minute by the compaction loop in `db.go:993-1027`\n- Runs when the head block is \"compactable\" (older than `chunkRange/2`)\n- Ensures timely persistence of in-memory data to disk\n\n**2. Size-based Trigger**\n- Head block is compacted when it reaches a size threshold\n- Determined by `db.head.compactable()` check in `head.go`\n\n**3. Appender-based Trigger**\n- Triggered on `Appender.Commit()` if head is compactable\n- Provides immediate notification of compactable blocks\n\n**4. Tombstone Cleanup Trigger**\n- Blocks with >5% tombstones are automatically compacted to remove deleted series (line 281 in `compact.go`)\n- Saves disk space by eliminating deletion markers\n\n**5. Overlapping Blocks Trigger**\n- If blocks overlap, they are immediately compacted together for correctness\n- Prevents query inconsistencies from overlapping time ranges\n\n### Compaction Process Flow\n\n```\n1. Trigger (time, size, or tombstone threshold)\n   ↓\n2. Acquire Compaction Mutex (cmtx)\n   ↓\n3. Compact Head Block (if compactable)\n   a. Create RangeHead wrapping the head\n   b. Write head to disk as level-1 block\n   c. Reload blocks and delete parents\n   ↓\n4. Compact Disk Blocks (multiple iterations)\n   a. Plan: Compactor.Plan() identifies compactable block groups\n   b. Compact: Merge identified blocks\n   c. Write: Create new compacted block\n   d. Reload: Update in-memory block list\n   e. Delete: Remove source blocks\n   ↓\n5. WAL Truncation (optional)\n   ↓\n6. Release Compaction Mutex\n```\n\n---\n\n## 2. Monitoring Indicators\n\n### Key Metrics to Watch\n\n#### Compaction Execution Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` | Counter | Total compactions executed | N/A (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` | Counter | Total triggered compactions | Increase rate >1/min may indicate high data churn |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` | Counter | Failed compactions (excluding cancellations) | **ALERT: ANY increase** indicates compaction failures |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` | Histogram | Time taken per compaction | p99 > 5min indicates slow compaction |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_populating_block` | Gauge | 1 = block being written, 0 = idle | Should be 0 most of the time |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_vertical_compactions_total` | Counter | Overlapping block compactions | High rate indicates frequent overlaps |\n\n#### Block and Storage Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` | Gauge | Number of on-disk blocks loaded in memory | >100 suggests compaction not keeping pace |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` | Gauge | Total on-disk block storage size | Compare to `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` | Gauge | Max bytes to retain (configured) | N/A (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_seconds` | Gauge | Max retention duration (configured) | N/A (informational) |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes` | Gauge | In-memory symbol table size | >500MB indicates many unique labels |\n\n#### Retention Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_time_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted due to time retention | Increase rate >0.5/hour may indicate aggressive retention |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_size_retentions_total` | Counter | Blocks deleted due to size retention | Increase indicates hitting size limits |\n\n#### Chunk Metrics (Level 1 compaction)\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_size_bytes` | Histogram | Final chunk size on first compaction | p50 < 100 bytes = inefficient chunking |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_samples` | Histogram | Samples per chunk on first compaction | p50 > 500 samples = good compression |\n| `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_chunk_range_seconds` | Histogram | Time range covered per chunk | Should align with scrape intervals |\n\n#### Tombstone Metrics\n\n| Metric | Type | Description | Alert Threshold |\n|--------|------|-------------|-----------------|\n| `prometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds` | Histogram | Time to recompact blocks and remove tombstones | p99 > 10min indicates heavy deletions |\n\n### Healthy Compaction Indicators\n\n✅ **Good signs:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` is **stable** (not increasing)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` p99 < 5 minutes\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` gradually increases then stabilizes after compaction\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` stays near configured retention limit\n- Compactions triggered roughly once per block duration (e.g., every 2 hours)\n\n### Unhealthy Compaction Indicators\n\n⚠️ **Warning signs:**\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` **increasing** → investigate logs\n- `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` **always increasing** → compaction not keeping pace\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` p99 > 10 minutes → system under stress\n- Logs showing \"compact %s: failed\" or \"compaction failed: %v\" → active failure\n- `prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes` exceeds `prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes` consistently\n\n### Alert Examples\n\n```yaml\n# Critical: Compaction Failures\n- alert: TSDBCompactionFailing\n  expr: rate(prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total[5m]) > 0\n  for: 10m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"Prometheus TSDB compaction failing on {{ $labels.job }}\"\n    description: \"Compactions have failed {{ $value }} times in last 5 minutes\"\n\n# Warning: Compaction Too Slow\n- alert: TSDBCompactionSlow\n  expr: histogram_quantile(0.99, prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds) > 300\n  for: 20m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"Prometheus TSDB compaction slow on {{ $labels.job }}\"\n    description: \"p99 compaction duration is {{ $value }}s (threshold: 300s)\"\n\n# Warning: Too Many Blocks\n- alert: TSDBTooManyBlocks\n  expr: prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded > 100\n  for: 30m\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"Too many blocks loaded on {{ $labels.job }}\"\n    description: \"{{ $value }} blocks loaded (compaction may not be keeping pace)\"\n\n# Warning: Storage Growing Beyond Retention\n- alert: TSDBSizeRetention\n  expr: prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes > prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes\n  for: 1h\n  annotations:\n    summary: \"TSDB storage exceeds retention limit on {{ $labels.job }}\"\n    description: \"Storage {{ $value }}B exceeds limit {{ $value }}B\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## 3. Failure Modes and Diagnostics\n\n### Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Prometheus crashes with \"no space left on device\" error\n- Compaction metrics stop updating\n- WAL or new blocks cannot be written\n- Logs show: `\"write merged meta: %w\"`, `\"sync temporary dir file: %w\"`, or `\"rename block dir: %w\"`\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total` increases sharply\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Retention settings too loose (time or size-based)\n- WAL not being truncated after compaction\n- Retention parameters misconfigured or not applied\n- Unexpected data ingestion spike\n- Other processes consuming disk space\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. **Check disk space:**\n   ```bash\n   df -h /prometheus-data-dir\n   du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/*\n   ```\n\n2. **Verify retention configuration:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect --metrics /prometheus-data-dir\n   # Look for block age and size\n   ls -lh /prometheus-data-dir | grep -E '^d' | head -20\n   ```\n\n3. **Check block metadata:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect --metrics /prometheus-data-dir | tail -20\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor compaction logs:**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch for \"compact blocks\" or \"compact blocks resulted in empty block\" messages\n   grep -i \"compact\\|delete\" /prometheus-logs/prometheus.log | tail -50\n   ```\n\n5. **Inspect WAL size:**\n   ```bash\n   du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/wal\n   du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/wbl  # Out-of-order WAL if present\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Block deletion logic: `tsdb/db.go:1652-1683` (deleteBlocks)\n- Retention enforcement: `tsdb/db.go:1568-1649` (deletableBlocks, BeyondTimeRetention, BeyondSizeRetention)\n- Compaction write: `tsdb/compact.go:606-717` (write function)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck / Not Progressing\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Compaction runs but never completes (hanging processes)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total` increases but `prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total` does not\n- Blocks accumulate; `prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded` continuously increases\n- Compaction log messages appear periodically but then stop\n- Out-of-memory errors or heavy CPU/disk I/O during compaction\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Compaction context cancelled due to shutdown or signal (lines 1158-1160 in db.go)\n- Query locks preventing block reloading after compaction\n- Corrupted block preventing reload (lines 1441-1477 in db.go)\n- Insufficient memory for merging large blocks\n- Disk I/O bottleneck causing timeout\n- Concurrent compaction mutex contention\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. **Check compaction loop status:**\n   ```bash\n   # Prometheus metrics endpoint\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep -i compaction\n   ```\n\n2. **Inspect goroutines and locks:**\n   ```bash\n   # Via pprof\n   curl -s http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/goroutine | head -100\n   curl -s http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/mutex | head -100\n   ```\n\n3. **Monitor block loading:**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch for reloadBlocks errors\n   grep -i \"reloadBlocks\\|failed to reloadBlocks\" /prometheus-logs/prometheus.log\n   ```\n\n4. **Check for corrupted blocks:**\n   ```bash\n   promtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data-dir 2>&1 | grep -i corrupt\n   # Or check each block's meta.json\n   for block in /prometheus-data-dir/*/meta.json; do\n     echo \"Checking $block\"\n     cat \"$block\" | jq .\n   done\n   ```\n\n5. **Monitor system resources:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check during compaction\n   top -b -n1 | grep prometheus\n   iostat -x 1 10\n   free -h\n   ```\n\n6. **Enable debug logging:**\n   ```bash\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/-/reload  # Reload config after adding debug level\n   # Or restart with --log.level=debug\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Compaction context handling: `tsdb/db.go:1008-1026`, `tsdb/compact.go:659-663`\n- Block reloading: `tsdb/db.go:1424-1529` (reloadBlocks)\n- Mutex locking: `tsdb/db.go:1134-1135` (Compact function lock)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption or Invalid Metadata\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Error messages: `\"Failed to read meta.json\"`, `\"corrupted block\"`, `\"unexpected meta file version\"`\n- Corrupted blocks marked for deletion but not fully removed\n- Queries fail with \"block not found\" or index corruption errors\n- `prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total` increments\n- Logs show: `\"Found corrupted block\"` (line 1474 in db.go)\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Disk corruption (bit rot, bad sector)\n- Abrupt process termination during block write (lines 712-715 in compact.go)\n- Filesystem error or unmapped device\n- Atomic rename failed (partial block write)\n- Incompatible version upgrade/downgrade\n- Manual block manipulation outside Prometheus\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. **List and inspect block metadata:**\n   ```bash\n   # Identify corrupted blocks\n   for block_dir in /prometheus-data-dir/*/; do\n     if ! cat \"$block_dir/meta.json\" 2>/dev/null | jq . >/dev/null; then\n       echo \"CORRUPTED: $(basename $block_dir)\"\n       ls -la \"$block_dir\"\n     fi\n   done\n   ```\n\n2. **Check filesystem integrity:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check for filesystem errors\n   fsck -n /dev/prometheus-device  # Read-only check\n   # Check if device is mounted read-only\n   mount | grep prometheus-data-dir\n   ```\n\n3. **Inspect block structure:**\n   ```bash\n   # For a suspect block\n   block_id=\"01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV\"\n   cd /prometheus-data-dir/$block_id\n   ls -la\n\n   # Check index file\n   file index\n\n   # Check chunks\n   ls -la chunks/\n\n   # Validate meta.json JSON syntax\n   jq . meta.json\n   ```\n\n4. **Check for incomplete compactions:**\n   ```bash\n   # Look for .tmp-for-creation or .tmp-for-deletion directories\n   find /prometheus-data-dir -name \"*tmp*\" -type d\n   # These should be cleaned up automatically; if they persist, manual cleanup needed\n   ```\n\n5. **Disk integrity test:**\n   ```bash\n   # Verify block files with checksums (if available)\n   cd /prometheus-data-dir\n   find . -type f -name \"index\" -o -name \"chunks/*\" | xargs md5sum > checksums.txt\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Meta file reading: `tsdb/block.go:247-262` (readMetaFile)\n- Meta file writing: `tsdb/block.go:264-299` (writeMetaFile)\n- Atomic block rename: `tsdb/compact.go:712-715` (fileutil.Replace)\n- Block opening: `tsdb/block.go:328-390` (OpenBlock)\n- Corruption detection: `tsdb/db.go:1463-1477` (corrupted blocks handling)\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM) During Compaction\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- Process killed by OS (exit code 137 on Linux)\n- Kernel logs show: `\"Killed process ... (prometheus) total-vm ... rss ...\"`\n- Sudden Prometheus restart with no error logs\n- Compaction metrics show spike in `prometheus_tsdb_compaction_duration_seconds` before crash\n- Large blocks fail to compact (e.g., blocks with millions of series)\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- Compacting very large blocks with millions of series (lines 729-800 in compact.go)\n- Symbol table loading consumes excessive memory (line 272-284 in db.go)\n- Index reader keeping all label pairs in memory\n- Chunk merging for overlapping blocks with duplicate data\n- System has insufficient RAM for Prometheus heap\n- Memory leak in chunk pool or block readers\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. **Monitor memory usage:**\n   ```bash\n   # Watch real-time memory\n   watch -n 5 'ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep'\n\n   # Get process memory stats\n   cat /proc/$(pgrep prometheus)/status | grep -E \"VmPeak|VmHWM|VmRSS\"\n   ```\n\n2. **Check block sizes before compaction:**\n   ```bash\n   # Find largest blocks\n   du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/*/ | sort -h | tail -10\n\n   # Inspect block metadata\n   for d in $(du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/*/ | sort -rh | head -5 | awk '{print $2}'); do\n     echo \"Block: $d\"\n     jq '.stats, .compaction.level' \"$d/meta.json\"\n   done\n   ```\n\n3. **Check symbol table size:**\n   ```bash\n   # Via metrics\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size\n\n   # Query the count of unique label combinations\n   promtool tsdb inspect --metrics /prometheus-data-dir | grep -i symbol\n   ```\n\n4. **Review Prometheus heap configuration:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check startup parameters\n   ps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\n\n   # Current memory limit\n   ulimit -m  # Memory limit\n   ulimit -v  # Virtual memory\n   ```\n\n5. **Analyze compaction targets:**\n   ```bash\n   # Simulate compaction planning\n   promtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data-dir\n   # Look for very large or high-level blocks that would be merged\n   ```\n\n6. **Enable memory profiling:**\n   ```bash\n   # Via pprof\n   curl -s http://localhost:6060/debug/pprof/heap > heap.prof\n   go tool pprof heap.prof\n   # In pprof: top10, list [function_name]\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- Block population (merging): `tsdb/compact.go:729-850` (PopulateBlock)\n- Symbol table loading: `tsdb/db.go:272-284` (symbol table metrics)\n- Index reading: `tsdb/index/` package\n- Chunk pool management: `tsdb/chunkenc/pool.go`\n\n---\n\n### Failure Mode 5: WAL Truncation Failure\n\n**Symptoms:**\n- WAL directory grows unboundedly (`/prometheus-data-dir/wal` > 5GB)\n- `prometheus_tsdb_wal_corruptions_total` increases (indicates potential corruption)\n- Logs show: `\"WAL truncation in Compact\"`, `\"truncate WAL: %w\"`\n- Startup takes increasingly long (WAL replay is slow)\n- Metrics show normal compaction but WAL not being cleaned\n\n**Root Causes:**\n- WAL segments locked by concurrent readers (line 1147 in db.go)\n- Permission issues on WAL directory\n- Out-of-order head compaction preventing WAL truncation (lines 1205-1209 in db.go)\n- Last block max time not advancing (broken compaction chain)\n- Concurrent checkpoint/truncation operations\n\n**Diagnostic Steps:**\n\n1. **Check WAL directory size:**\n   ```bash\n   du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/wal\n   ls -lh /prometheus-data-dir/wal | head -20\n\n   # Count WAL segments\n   ls /prometheus-data-dir/wal | wc -l\n   # Expected: ~3-5 files; >10 indicates truncation failure\n   ```\n\n2. **Inspect WAL file locks:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check open file handles\n   lsof | grep prometheus | grep wal\n\n   # Check memory-mapped files\n   cat /proc/$(pgrep prometheus)/maps | grep wal\n   ```\n\n3. **Verify block time progression:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check newest block's MaxTime\n   latest_block=$(ls -1 /prometheus-data-dir | grep -v wal | grep -v wbl | sort -r | head -1)\n   cat /prometheus-data-dir/$latest_block/meta.json | jq '.maxTime'\n\n   # Compare with expected time (should be recent)\n   echo \"Current time (ms): $(date +%s)000\"\n   ```\n\n4. **Monitor OOO head compaction:**\n   ```bash\n   # Check if OOO head compaction is blocked\n   curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep -i \"out_of_order\"\n\n   # Look for OOO blocks\n   ls /prometheus-data-dir/*/meta.json | xargs grep -l \"from-out-of-order\"\n   ```\n\n5. **Check filesystem and permissions:**\n   ```bash\n   ls -ld /prometheus-data-dir/wal\n   # Should show: drwx------ prometheus prometheus\n\n   # Test write permission\n   touch /prometheus-data-dir/wal/test && rm /prometheus-data-dir/wal/test\n   ```\n\n**Code References:**\n- WAL truncation in compaction: `tsdb/db.go:1147-1150`, `tsdb/db.go:1192-1194`\n- OOO head compaction: `tsdb/db.go:1238-1283`\n- Head truncation: `tsdb/head.go` (head.truncateWAL method)\n\n---\n\n## 4. Recovery Procedures\n\n### Recovery Procedure for Failure Mode 1: Disk Space Exhaustion\n\n**Step 1: Stop Prometheus immediately**\n```bash\n# Gracefully shut down Prometheus to prevent data loss\n# If possible, give it 30 seconds to finish current operations\nkill -SIGTERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 30\n\n# If not stopping, force kill\nkill -SIGKILL $(pgrep prometheus)\n```\n\n**Step 2: Assess free disk space**\n```bash\ndf -h /prometheus-data-dir\n# Need at least 5GB free to safely restart compaction\ndu -sh /prometheus-data-dir/*\n```\n\n**Step 3: Delete old blocks manually if needed (last resort)**\n```bash\n# List blocks sorted by age (oldest first)\nls -lt /prometheus-data-dir | grep -v wal | grep -v wbl | tail -20\n\n# Identify ULID of oldest block to delete\noldest_block=\"01ARZ3NDEKTSV4RRFFQ69G5FAV\"\n\n# Delete with atomic rename pattern (safe)\nmv /prometheus-data-dir/$oldest_block /prometheus-data-dir/${oldest_block}.tmp-for-deletion\nrm -rf /prometheus-data-dir/${oldest_block}.tmp-for-deletion\n\n# Verify deletion\nls /prometheus-data-dir/$oldest_block 2>&1 | grep \"No such file\"\n\n# Repeat for multiple blocks as needed\n```\n\n**Step 4: Clean up orphaned temporary directories**\n```bash\n# Remove any incomplete compaction artifacts\nfind /prometheus-data-dir -name \"*tmp*\" -type d -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null || true\n```\n\n**Step 5: Adjust retention if needed**\n```bash\n# Update prometheus.yml retention settings:\n# storage:\n#   tsdb:\n#     retention.time: 7d        # Reduce from 15d to 7d\n#     retention.size: 50GB      # Add or reduce size-based limit\n\n# Then reload:\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:9090/-/reload\n```\n\n**Step 6: Restart Prometheus**\n```bash\n# Start with reduced retention temporarily\nprometheus --storage.tsdb.retention.time=7d --storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus-data-dir\n\n# Monitor startup logs\n# Watch for: \"completed write to block\" messages indicating compaction\n```\n\n**Step 7: Monitor compaction and disk space**\n```bash\n# Terminal 1: Watch metrics\nwatch -n 10 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep -E \"compactions|blocks|storage\"'\n\n# Terminal 2: Watch disk space\nwatch -n 10 'df -h /prometheus-data-dir && echo \"---\" && du -sh /prometheus-data-dir/*/ | sort -h'\n\n# Terminal 3: Monitor logs\ntail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -i \"compact\\|delete\\|retain\"\n```\n\n**Step 8: Verify recovery**\n```bash\n# Check that compactions are progressing\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n\n# Verify storage is decreasing\nwatch -n 60 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes'\n\n# Ensure no failures\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total\n# Should show 0 or stable value\n```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery Procedure for Failure Mode 2: Compaction Stuck\n\n**Step 1: Identify if compaction is truly stuck**\n```bash\n# Check if metrics are updating\nfor i in {1..5}; do\n  curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total\n  sleep 10\ndone\n# If value doesn't change, compaction is stuck\n\n# Check if Prometheus process is running\nps aux | grep prometheus | grep -v grep\npgrep -f prometheus\n```\n\n**Step 2: Attempt graceful shutdown with timeout**\n```bash\n# Send SIGTERM and wait\ntimeout 60 bash -c 'kill -SIGTERM $(pgrep prometheus) && wait $(pgrep prometheus)'\n\n# If timeout expires, process is hung - force kill\nif [ $? -eq 124 ]; then\n  kill -SIGKILL $(pgrep prometheus)\n  sleep 5\nfi\n```\n\n**Step 3: Check for incomplete compactions**\n```bash\n# Look for blocks in tmp directories (incomplete writes)\nfind /prometheus-data-dir -name \"*tmp*\" -type d -ls\n\n# Check if any .tmp-for-creation or .tmp-for-deletion directories exist\nls -la /prometheus-data-dir/*tmp* 2>/dev/null || echo \"No tmp directories found\"\n```\n\n**Step 4: Validate block metadata integrity**\n```bash\n# For each block, validate meta.json\nerrors=0\nfor block in /prometheus-data-dir/*/; do\n  if [ -f \"$block/meta.json\" ]; then\n    if ! jq . \"$block/meta.json\" >/dev/null 2>&1; then\n      echo \"INVALID JSON: $(basename $block)\"\n      ((errors++))\n    fi\n  fi\ndone\n\nif [ $errors -gt 0 ]; then\n  echo \"Found $errors blocks with invalid meta.json\"\n  # Proceed to Failure Mode 3 recovery\nelse\n  echo \"All block metadata valid\"\nfi\n```\n\n**Step 5: Restart Prometheus with compaction disabled (if needed)**\n```bash\n# Use this only if compaction causes repeated hangs\nprometheus \\\n  --storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus-data-dir \\\n  --storage.tsdb.allow-overlapping-blocks \\\n  > /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log 2>&1 &\n\n# Wait for startup\nsleep 30\n\n# Verify it stays alive\nsleep 30 && pgrep -f prometheus >/dev/null && echo \"Prometheus running\"\n```\n\n**Step 6: Manually trigger compaction with timeout**\n```bash\n# If Prometheus is running, try triggering via API\n# (Note: may not be available in all versions, check documentation)\n\n# Alternative: Restart to force compaction loop\nkill -SIGTERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 60\n\n# Start normally\nprometheus --storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus-data-dir &\n\n# Monitor with timeout\ntimeout 600 bash -c 'while true; do\n  compacted=$(curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics 2>/dev/null | grep prometheus_tsdb_compactions_total | grep -oE \"[0-9]+$\")\n  [ -n \"$compacted\" ] && echo \"Last compaction: $compacted\"\n  sleep 30\ndone'\n```\n\n**Step 7: If still stuck after restart, use promtool**\n```bash\n# Stop Prometheus\nkill -SIGTERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 10\n\n# Run promtool to check and repair\npromtool tsdb inspect /prometheus-data-dir\n\n# If errors found, attempt repair\npromtool tsdb repair /prometheus-data-dir\n\n# Then restart\nprometheus --storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus-data-dir &\n```\n\n**Step 8: Monitor and verify**\n```bash\n# Watch compaction progress\nwatch -n 30 'curl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep -E \"compactions_total|blocks_loaded|compaction_duration\"'\n\n# Check logs for errors\ntail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -i \"compact\\|error\"\n```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery Procedure for Failure Mode 3: Block Corruption\n\n**Step 1: Identify corrupted blocks**\n```bash\n# Full validation of all blocks\ncorrupted_blocks=()\nfor block_dir in /prometheus-data-dir/*/; do\n  [ -d \"$block_dir\" ] || continue\n\n  block_id=$(basename \"$block_dir\")\n\n  # Skip wal and wbl directories\n  [[ \"$block_id\" == \"wal\" || \"$block_id\" == \"wbl\" ]] && continue\n\n  # Validate meta.json\n  if ! jq . \"$block_dir/meta.json\" >/dev/null 2>&1; then\n    echo \"CORRUPTED meta.json: $block_id\"\n    corrupted_blocks+=(\"$block_id\")\n  fi\n\n  # Validate index file exists and is readable\n  if [ ! -f \"$block_dir/index\" ]; then\n    echo \"MISSING index: $block_id\"\n    corrupted_blocks+=(\"$block_id\")\n  fi\n\n  # Validate chunks directory\n  if [ ! -d \"$block_dir/chunks\" ]; then\n    echo \"MISSING chunks directory: $block_id\"\n    corrupted_blocks+=(\"$block_id\")\n  fi\ndone\n\necho \"Corrupted blocks: ${#corrupted_blocks[@]}\"\n```\n\n**Step 2: Stop Prometheus**\n```bash\n# Graceful shutdown\nkill -SIGTERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 30\n\n# If not stopped, force kill\npgrep -f prometheus && kill -SIGKILL $(pgrep prometheus)\n```\n\n**Step 3: Backup corrupted blocks**\n```bash\n# Create backup before deletion\nmkdir -p /backup/prometheus-corrupted-blocks-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)\nbackup_dir=/backup/prometheus-corrupted-blocks-$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)\n\nfor block_id in \"${corrupted_blocks[@]}\"; do\n  echo \"Backing up $block_id\"\n  cp -r /prometheus-data-dir/$block_id $backup_dir/\ndone\n\necho \"Backed up to: $backup_dir\"\n```\n\n**Step 4: Delete corrupted blocks safely**\n```bash\n# Use atomic rename pattern\nfor block_id in \"${corrupted_blocks[@]}\"; do\n  echo \"Deleting $block_id\"\n\n  # Create atomic deletion marker\n  mv /prometheus-data-dir/$block_id /prometheus-data-dir/${block_id}.tmp-for-deletion 2>/dev/null || {\n    # If rename fails, the block may be in use or inaccessible\n    echo \"Failed to rename $block_id, trying direct delete\"\n    rm -rf /prometheus-data-dir/$block_id\n    continue\n  }\n\n  # Remove the marked directory\n  rm -rf /prometheus-data-dir/${block_id}.tmp-for-deletion\n\n  echo \"Deleted: $block_id\"\ndone\n```\n\n**Step 5: Clean up temporary directories**\n```bash\n# Remove any remaining tmp artifacts\nfind /prometheus-data-dir -name \"*tmp*\" -type d -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null || true\n\necho \"Cleanup complete\"\n```\n\n**Step 6: Restart Prometheus**\n```bash\n# Start Prometheus - it will rebuild block list from remaining blocks\nprometheus --storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus-data-dir > /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log 2>&1 &\n\n# Monitor startup\nsleep 30\npgrep -f prometheus >/dev/null && echo \"Prometheus started\" || echo \"Failed to start\"\n\n# Watch for reloadBlocks operations\ntail -f /var/log/prometheus/prometheus.log | grep -i \"reload\"\n```\n\n**Step 7: Verify recovery**\n```bash\n# Check that Prometheus is queryable\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/-/healthy\n# Should return \"Prometheus is healthy\"\n\n# Verify block count is reduced\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_blocks_loaded\n\n# Check for ongoing errors\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/metrics | grep prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures\n# Should not increment\n```\n\n**Step 8: Restore from backup if needed**\n```bash\n# If data loss is unacceptable, restore from backup or replication:\n# - Restore backup from cloud storage (S3, GCS, etc.)\n# - Fail over to replicated instance\n# - Contact your backup/replication provider\n\n# If local backup is usable:\n# stop Prometheus\nkill -SIGTERM $(pgrep prometheus)\nsleep 30\n\n# Restore specific blocks\ncp -v /backup/prometheus-corrupted-blocks-XXX/* /prometheus-data-dir/\n\n# Restart\nprometheus --storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus-data-dir &\n```\n\n---\n\n### Recovery Procedure for Failure Mode 4: Out-of-Memory (OOM)\n\n**Step 1: Confirm OOM kill occurred**\n```bash\n# Check system logs\ndmesg | tail -20 | grep -i \"killed\\|oom\"\n\n# On systemd\njournalctl -u prometheus -n 50 --no-pager\n\n# On docker/kubernetes\ndocker logs <container_id> | tail -50\nkubectl logs <pod_name> -n prometheus | tail -50\n```\n\n**Step 2: Increase system memory (if possible)**\n```bash\n# Option A: Vertical scaling - add more RAM to the system\n# This is the simplest solution if infrastructure allows\n\n# Option B: Enable swap (temporary workaround)\n# WARNING: Swap is much slower than RAM\nfallocate -l 8G /swap-file\nchmod 600 /swap-file\nmkswap /swap-file\nswapon /swap-file\n# Add to /etc/fstab for persistence\n\n# Option C: Limit Prometheus heap size explicitly\n# Edit systemd service or docker config:\n# prometheus --storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus-data-dir -mem-limit=8GB\n# (Note: actual flag may vary; check Prometheus version)\n```\n\n**Step 3: Reduce retention to lower memory footprint**\n```bash\n# Update prometheus.yml:\n# storage:\n#   tsdb:\n#     retention.time: 7d         # Reduce from 15d to 7d\n#     retention.size: 25GB       # Lower size limit\n#     max-block-duration: 24h    # Increase to reduce total blocks\n\n# Update in config file\ncat > /etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml << 'EOF'\nglobal:\n  scrape_interval: 15s\nstorage:\n  tsdb:\n    retention.time: 7d\n    retention.size: 25GB\n    max-block-duration: 24h\n# ... rest of config\nEOF\n```\n\n**Step 4: Identify and exclude high-cardinality metrics (if applicable)**\n```bash\n# Find metrics with high cardinality\npromtool tsdb inspect --metrics /prometheus-data-dir | grep -i cardinality\n\n# Or query running Prometheus\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=count(%7B__name__=~%22.*%22%7D) | jq\n\n# Identify problematic metric families\ncurl -s http://localhost:9090/api/v1/query?query=count(count(%7B__name__=%22metric_name%22%7D)%20by%20(label)) | jq\n\n# Add relabeling to drop high-cardinality labels (in prometheus.yml):\n# Code Reference\n\n### Key Functions by Failure Mode\n\n#### Disk Space Exhaustion\n- **Block deletion**: `tsdb/db.go:1652-1683` - `deleteBlocks()`\n- **Retention calculation**: `tsdb/db.go:1568-1649` - `deletableBlocks()`, `BeyondTimeRetention()`, `BeyondSizeRetention()`\n- **Compaction write**: `tsdb/compact.go:606-717` - `write()` method\n- **Block atomicity**: `tsdb/block.go:264-299` - `writeMetaFile()`\n\n#### Compaction Stuck\n- **Compaction loop**: `tsdb/db.go:993-1027` - main compaction loop with triggering\n- **Mutex handling**: `tsdb/db.go:1134-1135` - `Compact()` lock acquisition\n- **Context cancellation**: `tsdb/db.go:1158-1160` - context cancel handling\n- **Block reload**: `tsdb/db.go:1424-1529` - `reloadBlocks()`\n\n#### Block Corruption\n- **Meta file reading**: `tsdb/block.go:247-262` - `readMetaFile()`\n- **Meta file writing**: `tsdb/block.go:264-299` - `writeMetaFile()`\n- **Block opening**: `tsdb/block.go:328-390` - `OpenBlock()`\n- **Atomic rename**: `tsdb/compact.go:712-715` - `fileutil.Replace()`\n\n#### Out-of-Memory\n- **Block population**: `tsdb/compact.go:729-850` - `PopulateBlock()`\n- **Symbol table**: `tsdb/db.go:272-284` - symbol table metrics and loading\n- **Chunk merging**: `tsdb/compact.go:800-850` - merging chunks in compaction\n\n#### WAL Truncation\n- **WAL truncation**: `tsdb/db.go:1147-1150`, `1192-1194` - WAL truncation calls\n- **OOO compaction**: `tsdb/db.go:1238-1283` - `compactOOOHead()`\n- **Head truncation**: `tsdb/head.go` - `truncateWAL()` and `truncateMemory()` methods\n\n### Important Types and Constants\n\n```go\n// Block metadata structure (tsdb/block.go:162-179)\ntype BlockMeta struct {\n    ULID        ulid.ULID\n    MinTime, MaxTime int64\n    Stats       BlockStats\n    Compaction  BlockMetaCompaction\n    Version     int\n}\n\n// Compaction metadata (tsdb/block.go:196-212)\ntype BlockMetaCompaction struct {\n    Level      int         // 1, 2, 3, ... ($i/30)\"\n    sleep 10\ndone\n\necho \"Recovery complete. Backup saved to: $BACKUP_DIR\"\n```\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThis runbook provides operational guidance for managing Prometheus TSDB compaction in production.
